# Oracle — Hourly Improvement Worklog

This file is the shared memory for the hourly scheduled task. Each run is a fresh
session with NO memory of prior runs, so this log is the ONLY continuity between them.
Every run MUST read this file first and append to it last.

## Current state (seed)
- File under work: `index.html` (single-file, static, GitHub Pages compatible)
- Build tag at seed: `v4.14 · 2026-07-16`
- Commanders in STUDY_DB at seed: ~55
- Seeded: 2026-07-17 01:23 EDT

## Focus rotation
Runs alternate between two focus modes. Read `NEXT FOCUS` below to decide this run's mode.
- **LOGIC** run: study one new commander, verify the RAILS engine + parameter transforms
  handle it correctly, audit per-rail Scryfall result quality, fix real bugs.
- **UI** run: improve visual design, responsiveness, usability, organization, polish —
  inspired by GOAT, Moxfield, VS Code, Cities: Skylines, Steam, Discord,
  Star Wars Battlefront II, Apple Music, Spotify.

**NEXT FOCUS: UI**

REVIEWED live in Chrome across Search landing, Deck, Shop, Workshop synergy rails, and card detail (published v4.39→v4.40 during the run). Found a real inconsistency in hover affordance: the Workshop's `.syn-card` synergy tiles lift + shadow + border-glow on desktop hover (L760), but the app's TWO most-browsed grids stayed dead flat — the main search results `.card-tile` had only a tiny image `scale(1.025)` (L765) and NO card lift, and the Similar-commanders `.sim-card` had NO transition, NO hover, NO :active at all. FIX (surgical, CSS-only, mirrors the proven syn-card recipe): (1) `.card-tile` base transition `transform .12s, box-shadow .15s` → `transform .3s var(--spring), box-shadow .3s ease, border-color .2s ease` (matches syn-card's spring feel; border-color now eases so the in-deck gold edge fades in instead of snapping). (2) `.sim-card` base: added the same transition + `.sim-card:active{scale(.97)}` (tap parity) + `.sim-img img{transition:transform .35s var(--fluid)}`. (3) In the EXISTING `@media (hover:hover) and (pointer:fine)` block (so mobile/touch is 100% untouched — no sticky-tap hover): `.card-tile:hover` and `.sim-card:hover` get `translateY(-4px) + 0 16px 32px rgba(0,0,0,.5) shadow + border-color rgba(224,196,106,.42)` gold edge; `.card-tile.in-deck:hover` composes the lift shadow WITH the in-deck gold ring (`,0 0 0 1px rgba(224,196,106,.45)`) so an in-deck card keeps its ring while lifting; `.sim-card:hover .sim-img img{scale(1.03)}` adds a slow Ken-Burns zoom (the search grid already had its `.card-img-wrap:hover img` zoom, now paired with a lift). All new colors reuse the file's gold triplet; var(--spring)/(--fluid) are used before their :root decl exactly like the existing syn-card L679 (custom props are order-independent). Inherits the global prefers-reduced-motion neutralizer (L642) for free, same as syn-card. No JS, no new dependency, no per-frame work — pure GPU transform/opacity/shadow, zero perf impact, zero functionality change (constraint 3/4/5). VISUAL VERIFICATION via Chrome (extension connected): ran a Board Wipes search (96 `.card-tile`s), injected the byte-identical CSS, force-applied the hover state to a loaded tile (Abu Ja'far) and zoom-compared against its unlifted neighbor — tile raises, art scales edge-to-edge, gold edge lights, neighbors + layout unaffected. | 28 | 2026-07-17 16:05 EDT | POLISH | — | Backup: index-backup-20260717-1602.html. VISUAL FLAIR / discoverability (the "what would Apple Music/Spotify do" kind). REVIEWED live in Chrome (Search landing, results, Deck, Workshop synergy, card detail; published v4.40). Found the app's FRONT-DOOR affordance gap: the top filter chip row (`.chip-row` — All · Legendaries · Creatures · Instants · Sorceries · Enchant. · Artifacts · Walkers · Lands) is `overflow-x:auto` with BOTH `scrollbar-width:none` and a hidden webkit scrollbar, so on desktop AND mobile the overflowing chips (measured live: scrollWidth 732 vs clientWidth 556 at a 1100px window) were CHOPPED FLAT at the container edge with zero hint the row scrolls — "Artifac…" cut mid-word, looking like the list ended there. Every other scroller in the file either shows a thin desktop scrollbar (screen/synergy-scroll/sheet-body, v-prior) or is short enough not to matter; the chip row was the one high-traffic horizontal scroller with no cue. FIX (surgical: 1 ref + 1 useEffect + 3 CSS rules, mask-based, zero DOM restructuring): a scroll-position-aware EDGE FADE — CSS `mask-image`/`-webkit-mask-image` linear-gradient(90deg…) fades whichever edge still hides content, keyed off a `data-ef` attribute the JS sets to `s` (at start → fade right 26px), `m` (middle → fade both), `e` (at end → fade left), or removes entirely when the row doesn't overflow. Wired ONLY to the single `.chip-row` via a new `chipRowRef` + a self-contained useEffect in SearchScreen: an `apply()` reads scrollWidth/clientWidth/scrollLeft (2px threshold) and sets/clears `data-ef`; a passive `scroll` listener + `window resize` listener both feed a single rAF-coalesced scheduler (no polling, no per-frame work — fires only on real scroll/resize); an extra post-mount rAF re-measures after font/layout settle; cleanup removes both listeners + cancels the rAF. The mask is horizontal-only (90deg) so it never clips vertical content — deliberately chosen over the hover-lifting card rails (`.synergy-rail` has v4.41 translateY(-4px) tiles whose top edge a mask box COULD clip), which is why this run scoped the fade to the text-pill chip row only (no vertical overflow risk) and left the card rails as a future candidate needing a wrapper-overlay approach instead of an element mask. No capability touched: all 9 chips in the same positions, same taps, same active-gold state; purely how the row's edges are painted. VISUAL VERIFICATION via Chrome (extension connected): injected the byte-identical CSS + the exact apply() logic onto the live published chip row and screenshotted all three states — start: "All" solid at left, "Artifacts" softly fading at right (vs the hard v4.40 cut); middle (scrollLeft 90): "…ndaries" fading in at left AND "Walker…" fading out at right; end (scrollLeft=scrollWidth): logic returns `e` → left-only fade — every chip still readable, layout byte-identical, nothing else on the page moved. Validation: 5/5 script blocks `node --check` (fresh /tmp/orv442); style braces balanced 806/806 (+3 pairs = 3 new rules); CRLF intact (4994 pairs, 0 lone LF, raw-byte check); meta===CHANGELOG[0]===v4.42; `chip-row[data-ef` appears 3× (3 states), `chipRowRef` 3× (useRef decl + ref prop + effect). Focus = UI per NEXT FOCUS marker. SHIPPED **SEARCH-BOX ENTER RACE FIX** — a real, reproducible defect on the app's front door (the north-star's commander/card discovery entry point). IN-BROWSER REPRO on the now-matching deployed v4.78 (extension can finally review the shipping build directly instead of injecting onto stale v4.60): clicked the search box, typed 'Korvold', waited 1s (warm), pressed Enter → the network log showed the request was `q=game%3Apaper&order=name&unique=cards` — the bare EVERYTHING search (32,416 cards A–Z: Aang, Aardvark, Abaddon…), NOT Korvold; confirmed the DOM input.value was 'Korvold' at the time, proving Enter searched a stale/empty React `query` state instead of the box's actual contents. ROOT CAUSE: the input's onKeyDown Enter handler called `doSearch()` with NO queryOverride, so doSearch read `raw = query.trim()` from the useCallback closure `[query,…]`; when the committed React state lags the visible box (cold first submit, fast typing, or paste-then-Enter — exactly the transient run 63 flagged 'low-priority for a UI run to guard doSearch against empty-raw on first submit'), raw is '' and doSearch falls through to its `|| 'game:paper'` everything-branch. FIX (surgical, ~6 lines, one call site): the Enter handler now captures `const v = e.target.value` (the LIVE box contents) and calls `setQuery(v)` + `doSearch({ queryOverride: v })`, so Enter always searches exactly what's on screen, immune to the state-commit race — the autocomplete-select, chip, filter, inject, and `/`-shortcut paths already passed explicit overrides and were untouched. VALIDATION: 5/5 script blocks node --check (fresh mktemp); node harness (7/7) on the exact doSearch query-builder proving the OLD stale-state path yields 'game:paper' while the NEW queryOverride path yields 'Korvold game:paper' (+ regressions: warm case, empty-box unchanged, chip-scoped submit, raw-syntax query, no game:paper double-append when in:/game: present); END-TO-END on live Scryfall the fixed query 'Korvold game:paper' returns 3 Korvold cards (not 32,416). No CSS/markup change (pure behavior), so zero responsive/visual regression risk — style braces 990/990 unchanged, mobile deterministically identical. Fixed a pre-existing version drift while here: the console banner was stuck at v4.77 while meta/CHANGELOG were v4.78 — all four refs now read v4.79 · 2026-07-23.
